< Review>
If you're looking for a trustworthy place to take your car for maintenance or repairs, look no further. Kim went above and beyond to help me when I brought I my car in with multiple repairs and maintenance needs. Here are just a few of the things that really set Miramar Automotive & Transmission apart from other shops I've taken my car into:

1) Kim and her team gave me regular updates on the status of my car.

They provided me with a report with pictures of each aspect of my car. This included items like the color, pH, and fill-level of my coolant, the condition of my air filter, and the condition of my tires, etc.

2) They were thorough with their work

During their inspection they noticed some liquid had splattered inside of my engine bay. It turned out this was the symptom of an issue with my motor mount. They included those pictures in my report and helped me find an issue with my car that I didn't know I had!

I've taken my car to OTHER shops in the past where they claimed a "100-point inspection" that included checking my reverse lights. All those other shops claimed that they had checked them and they were fine. Well they were broken (I had known it for a while), so I know that they didn't actually check. Kim's team was the only one that ever caught my lights being out.

3) Kim helped me avoid doing repairs/maintenance that my car didn't need to save me money.

I had requested some maintenance that they found I didn't need. It ended up saving me $200!

Please keep in mind my car is like my baby to me so when I move to a new area it's very important that I find a shop that I know will take good care of it. Seriously, stop Google searching and just give them a call to schedule your appointment.

Thanks again Kim and Zach it was a pleasure doing business with you! I'll absolutely be back in the future.<//Review>

< review>
We are staying across at a resort across from this restaurant. They were highly recommended. So after swimming at the pool with the kids, I ordered online for pick up.

The place was packed. They distanced the tables from each other. The bar was full too. Maybe a few chairs here and there open.

It took a while for me to get my food. I‚Äôm standing in a corner and everyone keep asking me if I‚Äôm picking up for door dash. I‚Äôm not sure why they kept on saying that but it got to a point that it was irritating. I showed 3 people the receipt of my online order. I have them my name.

Finally, when my food came out the guy that brought it out asked if I‚Äôm with door dash again. I showed him my receipt and he said this is your food.

My mistake was not to check for utensils. I did mention to the manager that we are staying at the resort across the street. But the person that brought out the food was different. I had to eat the calamari with my hands until we were able to get fork and spoon from the front desk.

That‚Äôs the only reason why I gave a 4 star instead of 5.

For the food, it‚Äôs a 5 star all the way. The crust of the pizza is similar to the one I tried in Naples (de Michel), the calamari was perfectly cooked. Not to soft and not too chewy. The pasta was good as well.

If you are planning to stop by and try food here, come early and try to get a table. The location is nice too but parking could be a problem.< /review>

<text>I've been to this restaurant three times now. Every time I go, I bring more people with me. It's seriously WONDERFUL! Let's start with the location: perched on the edge of a lake, you feel like you're stepping into another world! There are swans lazily puttering around, a view of a small vineyard located on opposite side of the lake, and there are GONDOLAS on the water...GONDOLAS! It's amazing! I kept thinking, "Where even am I?"
Then there is the service: this is a family owned restaurant; an ITALIAN family owns and runs this place. They are the most welcoming, friendly and lively bunch I've ever had the pleasure of visiting! With the way they interact with one another, bantering in Italian; laughing and just enjoying each other as they serve their guests... It felt like these people REALLY, truly LOVE what they do; they love to serve and to feed and to connect with their guests. I felt like I was visiting them in one of their own homes. Everyone I have brought to Amalfi Cucina Italiana has raved about their experience.
Now for the food: this is LEGIT Italian food. I think the only thing more authentic would be to go to Italy herself...but maybe not even then. I heard that the chef who makes the pizzas is actually from the place in Italy where pizza was invented... Napoli? I have to be honest: I've only had the pizza here. I'm seriously ADDICTED to it. It's SOOOO good! The crust is like nothing I've had anywhere else. It's the perfect balance of soft, fluffy, doughy and crispy somehow. I don't know how they do it. I'm sure there is some sort of wizardry involved. I highly recommend the margherita pizza. One day I might try one of the other tempting dishes that I see come out of that kitchen. But for now, my heart is full with the most perfect pizza I've ever had.
This place is PERFECT for a casual date night, a special occasion, or just some friends and family getting together.
The upstairs, indoor dining area should be opening any day. I got to peek inside today and... Oh boy! I seriously want to move in to that place and call it home. Blue velvet sofas; gold mosaic pizza oven; purple orchids everywhere; fireplace; posh bar with wines and spirits galore; gorgeous view of the lake; incredible photographic art of different iconic Italian destinations grace the walls.
I cannot say enough good things about this place. I seriously want to be adopted into this family. I'm sure my actual parents would understand and agree with me. Please do yourself the biggest favor you'll ever do for yourself, and visit this restaurant!
Heads up: they don't require masks here. It's literally a breath of fresh air. The staff does not wear masks either. Life feels normal and happy here! If you prefer to wear a mask, that is okay. You will not be treated any differently. But if being around unmasked people makes you uncomfortable or makes you feel unsafe, you may want skip this place and visit your local Pizza Hut instead.<//text><pictures>None<//pictures><response>None</response><gmapID>0x80dc7574181e699b:0x2134439d831ade4e</gmapID></record>

<date>1613602353475</date><text>ITALIAN WINNER ! My wife and I are big fans of Italian food and in particular Buona Forchetta restaurants in San Diego. We were lucky to have a new Buona Forchetta open in Encinitas about 2 years ago...10 minutes from home. The amazing manager Giuseppe Annunziata made us feel so welcome that we practically lived there. But life goes on and Giuseppe got an offer he couldn't refuse.....to open his own restaurant right here. And so he did with 3 other Italian business partners ( former work colleagues at Buona Forchetta incl Executive Chef Marcello & Manager Emilio Muslija ). Amalfi Cucina Italiana ( named for the region Giuseppe came from in Italy ) opened it's doors on August 26th, 2020 smack in the middle of the covid shutdown. The amazing restaurant has 2 levels ( it was 2 separate eateries before )....a casual bar / eatery patio downstairs where we had lunch and a huge fine dining area upstairs with sensational panoramic views of Lake San Marcos. The upstairs dining area is still being renovated and should be ready in about 2 months. I contacted Giuseppe the co-owner a couple of weeks ago and said we must come for lunch...and catch up with our good friend. So on Thursday my wife and I arrived here around midday and found our way downstairs to the bar & casual dining patio overlooking Lake San Marcos. There were a few people enjoying drinks at the bar but not a lot going on. We found a table and checked out the lunch menu. I walked over to the cashier / hostess desk and ordered 2 x Lattes and a Mammamia ( Italian Sausage, Smoked Mozzarella, Red Bell Peppers, stuffed with Wedge Potatoes ) + a side of Marinara Sauce to share on 2 plates. The young female hostess named Maddie was very polite when I paid and I asked her to let our friend Giuseppe know we were here. Within a couple of minutes I spotted Giuseppe and he spotted me. I took him straight to chat with my wife....it was wonderful ! My wife and I know very little about dining in San Marcos and hardly ever visit the area. Simply knowing that an exceptional operator like Giuseppe is running the show is enough to put San Marcos in our dining loop. Manager Emilio ( one of the restaurant partners we know from Buona Forchetta ) came over to our table to say hi and take care of making our lattes. In the meantime Giuseppe brought us a couple of glasses of bubbly Prosecco and told us his exciting story about starting up the restaurant. We were so happy for him....such a talented restaurateur ! Our lunch order came out and looked quite remarkable...like a Calzone on steroids. They also call it a Pizza Sandwich. Anyway we each grabbed a slice and thought it tasted darn good particularly if the rich Marinara Sauce was poured over it. Our lattes arrived about the same time courtesy of Emilio one of the managers. Giuseppe excused himself as he had work to attend to but said he would love to show us the fine dining area upstairs before we left. We enjoyed our delicious lunch...the Mammamia was something new to us and very flavorsome. And our lattes were very well made and tasted wonderful. It certainly was a unique experience having lunch on Lake. San Marcos..water fountain, birdlife and gondolas. We headed upstairs after asking Maddie the hostess to grab Giuseppe for us. And what an amazing sight.....a huge gold colored Italian wood-fired oven greeted our eyes straight up..not in use yet for diners downstairs but it was fired up. A panoramic view of Lake San Marcos through lots of huge glass windows plus an enormous outdoor dining deck. A floor to ceiling fireplace near the entrance looked so inviting. I said to Giuseppe the dining area must be able to fit 200 people and he agreed. Of course when they open upstairs in a couple of months it will be 1/3 capacity due to covid restrictions. We can't wait to come back and enjoy dinner in the beautiful fine dining room. We think this Italian restaurant is going to be a huge success !</text>< name>

< Text>
First time here and in times of covid-19 they are doing a pretty good business. They don't have spaghetti or other pasta. Their special for the night had lasagna. They have quite a few pizzas and sandwiches. We had a pepperoni pizza and lasagna. The dishes were pretty good but you need to like thin wood fired type pizza. Not loaded with topping. It was freshly made though. I didn't have the lasagna but my husband and our guest said it was good but not great. My husband liked the Italian better over at eugenio's close by a few streets over. For dessert we had cannoli's and chocolate mousse. Very good! They so not have regular coffee and there's no decaf.....Only cappuccino and it's strong. My husband would have loved dinner decaf with dessert.
The setting is beautiful on the lake and will be interesting to see if the upstairs part does something different.
Staff is great! Service above and beyond tonight!< /Text>

<username>Virginia Campbell< /username>< text>
We have been looking for a speakeasy bar in the area and came across here. It's a hidden gem!! There are no signs, it's behind Vitello's restaurant (so you need to enter through there).

Check in the front and someone will take you to the back. You entered through a door and the room will take you back to the 1920's.  There are many seating options but we sat at the bar. We like to see the bartender in action. Scott, the bartender was so friendly and made the best drinks. We started with the Rendition old-fashioned and it did not disappoint. Then I asked for a custom drink, just let him know the base and your preference and he will make you a drink with it's own name. I love mezcal and no sweetness and he made me the perfect drink and named it the San Fernando.

It's a member bar but you can make reservations through yelp. They have magic Tuesday and we will definitely be going back.

You don't have to deal with crazy crowds, lines or rowdy people.

Make sure to ask for Scott!<//text>

Their records are unorganized, inaccurate, and incomplete to the point that their own representatives cannot find requested information.  If you have an issue with their services, the situation will not be resolved due to nonexistent customer service.  For example, let‚Äôs say you question a charge on your statement, you will: not be able to speak to the same person, have to repeat yourself multiple times, never receive any follow through/follow up, somehow finally confirm the issue was miraculously resolved only to receive a collections notice warning 2 months later, and have to start the process all over again.  At this point you are so beyond frustrated you pay the charge they cannot justify with proof just to not have to deal with the company any more.  That is how they get you, confusion and frustration.  What I would like to know is why cities keep awarding/renewing contracts to Republic Services.
